<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
II<br>
SERVICES TO BE PROVIDED</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Exhibits.</u></font></b></h2>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Exhibits&nbsp;1
through 6 (collectively, the &#147;Exhibits&#148;) attached to and made a part of this
Agreement describe the services to be provided by ALCS to Kraft and one or more
members of the Kraft Group, as designated from time to time by Kraft (the &#147;Transition
Services&#148; or &#147;Services&#148;).&#160; The Parties
have made a good faith effort as of the date hereof to identify each Transition
Service and to complete the content of the Exhibits accurately.&#160; It is anticipated that the Parties will
modify the Transition Services from time to time.&#160; In that case or to the extent that any
Exhibit is incomplete, the Parties will use good faith efforts to modify the
Exhibits.&#160; There are certain terms that
are specifically addressed in the Exhibits attached hereto that may differ from
the terms provided hereunder.&#160; In those
cases, the specific terms described in the Exhibits shall govern that
Transition Service.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; The Parties may also
identify additional Services that they wish to incorporate into this
Agreement.&#160; The Parties will create
additional Exhibits setting forth the description of such Services, the Fees
for such Services and any other applicable terms.</font></h3>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Independent Contractors.</u></font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ALCS will provide the
Transition Services either through its own resources, through the resources of
its subsidiaries or Affiliates, or by contracting with independent contractors
as agreed hereunder.&#160; To the extent that
ALCS decides to provide a Transition Service through an independent contractor
in the future, ALCS shall consult with and obtain the prior approval of Kraft,
which approval shall not be unreasonably withheld.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Standard of Care</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In providing the
Transition Services hereunder, ALCS will exercise the same degree of care as it
has historically exercised in providing such Transition Services to its
Affiliates prior to the date hereof, including at least the same level of
quality, responsiveness and timeliness as has been exercised by ALCS with
respect to such Transition Services.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Records</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ALCS shall keep full and
detailed records dealing with all aspects of the Transition Services performed
by it hereunder (the &#147;Records&#148;) and:</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; shall provide access
to the Records to Kraft at all reasonable times; and</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; shall maintain the
Records in accordance with good record management practices and with at least
the same degree of completeness and care as it maintains for its other similar
business interests.</font></h3>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
III<br>
FEES</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>General</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft will pay to ALCS a
fixed fee for each Transition Service as set forth in the attached Exhibits
(collectively, the &#147;Fees&#148;).&#160; The Fees
constitute full compensation to ALCS for all charges, costs and expenses
incurred by ALCS on behalf of Kraft in providing the Services, unless otherwise
specifically provided in the Exhibits.&#160;
Notwithstanding the terms of any of the Exhibits, the Fees for each
Transition Service shall be reduced by any amounts Kraft is required to pay
pursuant to <u>Section 3.1(e)</u> of the Employee Matters Agreement (the &#147;Employee
Matters Agreement&#148;), dated as of even date herewith, between Kraft and Altria,
with respect to any person who provides Services under this Agreement and
thereafter becomes a Kraft Transferee (as defined in the Employee Matters
Agreement).&#160; Except as specifically
provided herein or in the Exhibits, or as subsequently agreed by Kraft and
ALCS, Kraft will not be responsible to ALCS or any independent contractor
retained by ALCS, for any additional fees, charges, costs or expenses relating
to the Services, unless such additional fees, charges, costs or expenses are a
direct result of Kraft&#146;s unilateral deviation from the scope of the services
defined in the Exhibits.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Payments</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ALCS will deliver to Kraft, no later than five days
following the last day of each month, an invoice for the aggregate Fees
incurred for that month.&#160; Kraft will pay
to ALCS monthly no later than the third Wednesday of the following month, the
aggregate Fees incurred during the previous month.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
IV<br>
REPRESENTATIVES</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Representatives.</u></font></b></h2>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; The Controller of
Altria and the Controller of Kraft will serve as administrative representatives
(&#147;Representative(s)&#148;) of ALCS and Kraft, respectively, to facilitate day-to-day
communications and performance under this Agreement.&#160; Each Party may treat an act of a
Representative of the other Party as being authorized by such other Party.&#160; Each Party may replace its Representative by
giving written notice of the replacement to the other Party.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; No additional
Exhibits, modifications to existing Exhibits, or amendments to this Agreement
shall be effective unless and until executed by the Representatives of each of
ALCS and Kraft.</font></h3>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE V<br>
THIRD PARTY AGREEMENTS</font></b></h1>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the extent that it is
not practicable to have Kraft as the contracting Party for a third party obligation,
ALCS, with respect to all Services supplied by ALCS or contracted for by ALCS
on behalf of Kraft, shall use commercially reasonable efforts to cause all such
third party </font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\fc\899255154_H10375_1943966\9497-1-le.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 09:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">contracts to
extend to and be enforceable by Kraft, or to assign such contracts to
Kraft.&#160; In the event that such contracts
are not extendable or assignable, ALCS shall act as agent for Kraft in the
pursuit of any claims, issues, demands or actions against such third party
provider at Kraft&#146;s expense.&#160; Kraft will
indemnify ALCS for any liability under third party contracts arising directly
out of the acts or omissions of Kraft.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
VI<br>
AUTHORITY; INFORMATION; COOPERATION; CONSENTS</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Authority</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each Party represents to
the other Party that:</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; it has the requisite
corporate authority to enter into and perform this Agreement;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; its execution,
delivery and performance of this Agreement have been duly authorized by all
requisite corporate action on its behalf;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; this Agreement is
enforceable against it; and</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; it has obtained all
consents or approvals of Governmental Authorities and other Persons that are
conditions to its entering into this Agreement.</font></h3>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Information Regarding Transition
Services.</u></font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each Party shall make
available to the other Party any information required or reasonably requested
by that other Party regarding the performance of any Service and shall be
responsible for timely providing that information and for ensuring the accuracy
and completeness of that information; <u>provided</u>, <u>however</u>, that a
Party shall not be liable for not providing any information that is subject to
a confidentiality obligation owed by it to a Person other than an Affiliate of
it or the other Party.&#160; ALCS shall not be
liable for any impairment of any Service caused by ALCS not receiving information
from Kraft, either timely or at all, or by its receiving inaccurate or
incomplete information from Kraft, in each case that is required or reasonably
requested regarding that Service.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Cooperation</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Parties will
use good faith efforts to cooperate with each other in all matters relating to
the provision and receipt of Services.&#160;
Such good faith cooperation will include providing electronic access to
systems used in connection with Services and using commercially reasonable
efforts to obtain all consents, licenses, sublicenses or approvals necessary to
permit each Party to perform its obligations.&#160;
The Parties will cooperate with each other in making such information
available as needed in the event of any and all internal or external audits,
whether in the United States or any other country.&#160; If this Agreement is terminated in whole or
in part, the Parties will cooperate with each other in all reasonable respects
in order to effect an efficient transition and to minimize the disruption to the
business of both Parties, including the assignment or transfer of the rights
and obligations under any contracts.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='6',FILE='C:\fc\899255154_H10375_1943966\9497-1-le.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 09:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Further Assurances.</u></font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each Party shall
take such actions, upon request of the other Party and in addition to the
actions specified in this Agreement, as may be necessary or reasonably
appropriate to implement or give effect to this Agreement.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
VII<br>
AUTHORITY AS AGENT</font></b></h1>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ALCS is hereby authorized
to act as agent for Kraft for the purpose of performing Services hereunder and
as is necessary or desirable to perform such Services.&#160; Kraft will execute and deliver or cause the
appropriate member of the Kraft Group to execute and deliver to ALCS any
document or other evidence which may be reasonably required by ALCS to
demonstrate to third parties the authority of ALCS described in this <u>Article&nbsp;VII</u>.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
VIII<br>
CONFIDENTIAL INFORMATION</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Definition.</u></font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the purposes of this Agreement, &#147;Confidential
Information&#148; means non-public information about the disclosing Party&#146;s or any
of its Affiliates&#146; business or activities that is proprietary and confidential,
which shall include, without limitation, all business, financial, technical and
other information, including software (source and object code) and programming
code, of a Party or its Affiliates marked or designated &#147;confidential&#148; or &#147;proprietary&#148;
or by its nature or the circumstances surrounding its disclosure should
reasonably be regarded as confidential.&#160;
Confidential Information includes not only written or other tangible
information, but also information transferred orally, visually or
electronically or by any other means.&#160;
Confidential Information will not include information that (i)&nbsp;is
in or enters the public domain without breach of this Agreement, or (ii) the
receiving Party lawfully receives from a third party without restriction on
disclosure and, to the receiving Party&#146;s knowledge without breach of a
nondisclosure obligation.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Nondisclosure</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of ALCS and Kraft
agree that (i)&nbsp;it will not disclose to any third party or use any Confidential
Information disclosed to it by the other except as expressly permitted in this
Agreement, and (ii)&nbsp;it will take all reasonable measures to maintain the
confidentiality of all Confidential Information of the other Party in its
possession or control, which will in no event be less than the measures it uses
to maintain the confidentiality of its own information of similar type and
importance.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Permitted Disclosure</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notwithstanding the
foregoing, each Party may disclose Confidential Information (i)&nbsp;to the
extent required by a court of competent jurisdiction or other Governmental
Authority or otherwise as required by Law, including without limitation
disclosure obligations imposed under the federal securities laws, provided that
such Party has given the other Party prior notice of such </font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='7',FILE='C:\fc\899255154_H10375_1943966\9497-1-le.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 09:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">requirement when
legally permissible to permit the other Party to take such legal action to
prevent the disclosure as it deems reasonable, appropriate or necessary, or
(ii) on a &#147;need-to-know&#148; basis under an obligation of confidentiality to its
consultants, legal counsel, Affiliates, accountants, banks and other financing
sources and their advisors.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Ownership of Confidential
Information</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All Confidential
Information supplied or developed by either Party shall be and remain the sole
and exclusive property of the Party who supplied or developed it.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
IX<br>
TERM AND TERMINATION</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Term</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Agreement shall remain in effect until such time
as it has been terminated as to all Transition Services in accordance with <u>Section&nbsp;9.2</u>
hereof.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Termination</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Either Party may terminate this Agreement without
cause with respect to one or more Services under this Agreement by providing
three months&#146; written notice to the other Party or as otherwise agreed between
the Parties hereto; provided that the Services set forth in Exhibit 5 hereto
shall not terminate before December 31, 2007.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Termination Assistance Services</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ALCS agrees that, upon termination of this Agreement
or any of the Services set forth in the Exhibits, ALCS will cooperate in good
faith with Kraft to provide Kraft (or its designee) with reasonable assistance
to make an orderly transition from ALCS to another supplier of the
Services.&#160; Transition assistance services
shall include the following:</font></p>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; developing a
transition plan with assistance from Kraft or its designee;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; providing training
to Kraft personnel or its designee&#146;s personnel to perform Services; and</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; organizing and
delivering to Kraft records and documents necessary to allow continuation of
the Services, including delivering such materials in electronic forms and
versions as requested by Kraft.</font></h3>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE X<br>
LIMITATION OF LIABILITY; INDEMNIFICATION</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Limitation of Liability</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Except as may be provided
in <u>Section&nbsp;10.2</u> below and <u>Article V</u> above, ALCS and its
Affiliates (each, an &#147;ALCS Party&#148;) shall not be liable to any member of the
Kraft Group and its respective Affiliates (each, a &#147;Kraft Party&#148;) and each
Kraft Party shall not be liable to any ALCS Party, in each case, for any Losses
of a Kraft Party or an ALCS Party arising in connection with this Agreement and
the Services provided hereunder.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Indemnification</u>.</font></b></h2>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; ALCS shall
indemnify, defend and hold harmless each of the Kraft Parties from and against
all Losses, of any kind or nature, (i) incurred by a Kraft Party or (ii) of
third parties unrelated to any Kraft Party, in each case caused by or arising
in connection with the gross negligence or willful misconduct of any employee
of ALCS in connection with the performance of the Services, except to the
extent that the Losses were caused directly or indirectly by acts or omissions
of any Kraft Party.&#160; Notwithstanding the
foregoing, ALCS shall not be liable for any special, indirect, incidental, or
consequential damages relating to such claims.&#160;
Any Liability incurred by ALCS pursuant to this Agreement on or after
the Distribution Date shall be deemed to be an Altria Group Liability for
purposes of Article III of the Distribution Agreement.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:72.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Kraft shall
indemnify, defend and hold harmless each of the ALCS Parties from and against
all Losses of any kind or nature, (i) incurred by an ALCS Party or (ii) of
third parties unrelated to any ALCS Party, in each case caused by or arising in
connection with the gross negligence or willful misconduct of any employee of
Kraft in connection with Kraft&#146;s performance under this Agreement, except to
the extent that Losses were caused directly or indirectly by acts or omissions
of any ALCS Party.&#160; Notwithstanding the
foregoing, Kraft shall not be liable for any special, indirect, incidental, or
consequential damages relating to such claims.&#160;
Any Liability incurred by Kraft pursuant to this Agreement on or after
the Distribution Date shall be deemed to be a Kraft Group Liability for
purposes of Article III of the Distribution Agreement.</font></h3>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
XI<br>
DISPUTE RESOLUTION</font></b></h1>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Parties, or if the
Parties are unable to resolve any service or performance issues or if there is
a material breach of this Agreement that has not been corrected within thirty
(30) days of receipt of notice of such breach, the Controller and CFO of Kraft,
on behalf of Kraft, and the Treasurer and Controller of Altria, on behalf of
ALCS, will meet promptly to review and resolve those issues in good faith.</font></p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE
XII<br>
MISCELLANEOUS</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Original Services Agreement</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Agreement terminates
and supersedes the Original Services Agreement, which shall have no further
force and effect following the effectiveness of this Agreement.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Incorporation of Distribution
Agreement Provisions</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following provisions
of the Distribution Agreement are hereby incorporated herein by reference, and
unless otherwise expressly specified herein, such provisions shall apply as if
fully set forth herein (references in this <u>Section 12.2</u> to an &#147;Article&#148;
or &#147;Section&#148; shall mean Articles and Sections of the Distribution Agreement,
and except as expressly set forth below, references in the material
incorporated herein by reference shall be references to the Distribution
Agreement):&#160; Article III (relating to
Mutual Releases and Indemnification); Article IV (relating to certain
Additional Covenants); Article V (relating to Access to Information); and
Article IX (relating to Miscellaneous).</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Governing Law</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the extent not
preempted by applicable federal law, this Agreement shall be governed by,
construed and interpreted in accordance with the laws of the Commonwealth of
Virginia (other than the laws regarding the choice of laws and conflict of laws
as to all matters), including matters of validity, construction, effect,
performance and remedies <u>provided</u>, <u>however</u>, <u>that</u> the
Arbitration Act shall govern the matters described in Article X.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>References</u>.</font></b></h2>

<p align="left" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Except as provided in <u>Section 12.2</u> hereof all
references to Sections, Articles or Exhibits&#160;
contained herein mean Sections, Articles or Exhibits of or to this
Agreement, as the case may be, unless otherwise stated.</font></p>

<h2 style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.5.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Notices</u>.</font></b></h2>

notices and disclosures required or permitted by this Agreement shall be in

personally or by messenger or being received via telecopy, telex or other
electronic transmission, or two days after being sent by overnight delivery
service, in all cases addressed to the person for whom it is intended at the addresses
as follows:</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT
1</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CORPORATE
AFFAIRS SERVICES</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; GOVERNMENT AFFAIRS</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 90.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Lease of office space for Government
Affairs in the Washington DC location for no more than twelve months from March
30, 2007.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 83.95pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Fee payable for corporate affairs transition services shall include the monthly
rent of $69,610.00, based upon the ratio of the number of Kraft employees
utilizing the leased space divided by total occupants of the leased space times
the monthly rent and expenses.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.1</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 2</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">TREASURY SERVICES</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; RISK MANAGEMENT</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 84.25pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Consultation,
as requested by Kraft, on insurance renewals through November 1, 2007.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 84.25pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Maintenance
of and access to insurance claims data in connection with the agreement between
CS STARS LLC and ALCS, originally executed October 1, 2001.&#160; The estimated completion date for such
services is no later than October 1, 2007.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; BENEFIT INVESTMENTS</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 84.25pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Consultation,
as requested by Kraft, on administration of benefit trusts for a period of up
to six months after spin-off date.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Fee payable for the treasury transition services
for 2007 is based on the following:</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Risk Management &amp; Benefits Investments</font></i>.&#160; The Fee will include: (i) the relevant
Employee Costs associated with consultation time when requested; (ii) a
management fee equal to 5% of the aggregate amount calculated pursuant to (i);
and (iii) third-party expenses, including travel and entertainment and
consulting fees incurred on behalf of Kraft by ALCS.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.1</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FINANCIAL CONSOLIDATIONS &amp; REPORTING</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>FINANCIAL
CONSOLIDATIONS AND REPORTING</h3>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 83.95pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Review,

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Fee payable for the financial consolidations and
reporting transition services for 2007 shall include: (i) the relevant Employee
Costs associated with consultation time when requested; (ii) a management fee
equal to 5% of the aggregate amount calculated pursuant to (i); and (iii)
third-party expenses, including travel and entertainment, consulting fees and
printing costs incurred on behalf of Kraft by ALCS.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 4</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">INTERNAL AUDIT SERVICES</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 54.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Lease of office space in the United
Kingdom (5 Thameside Centre, Kew Bridge Road, London, TW8 0HF) until the
completion of Kraft&#146;s move to Zurich, Switzerland, estimated by June 30, 2007.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Fee payable for the
internal audit transition services for 2007 shall include: (i) the pro rata
amount of annual rent of $504,700 (GBP 272,800), based upon the number of
months Kraft employees occupy the London office space; (ii) the pro rata amount
of building services costs of $263,700 (GBP 142,500), based upon the number of
months Kraft employees occupy the London office space; and (iii) lease breakage
fee, if any.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 5</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">INFORMATION
TECHNOLOGY SERVICES</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Global
applications required by Kraft for business continuity (i.e. Global Treasury
and Global Network Services) will continue normal operations and provide
current services until the completion of Kraft&#146;s migration to EDS. The
estimated completion date for all services is no later than December 31, 2007.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Separation
of global applications, as identified in the current Business Restructure of
Systems and Services (&#147;Project BRASS&#148;) that have been agreed by ALCS and Kraft,
will incur costs until the full completion of Project BRASS, which will be
refined by ALCS and Kraft to ensure that the appropriate priorities are
established to achieve a completion date by December 31, 2007.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-30.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">C.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ALCS
Contracts Consulting services related to negotiation of separate enterprise
contracts between Kraft and major information technology vendors, including but
not limited to AT&amp;T, IBM, Oracle, Microsoft and SAP, including the
following actions:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 90.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Continue to communicate
to suppliers Altria&#146;s intent to separate global contracts and subsequently
receive written consents from the suppliers.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 72.0pt 12.0pt 90.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Track progress and
inform Kraft management of any potential service issues, cost impact or major
contractual challenges.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 72.0pt 12.0pt 90.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Ensure written closure,
including contractual sign-off with suppliers.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the event that Altria and Kraft do not complete all
required negotiations by December 31, 2007 and Kraft is still operating certain
software under an ALCS licensee, any third party fee incurred by Altria for
this continuation of service will be passed on to Kraft for appropriate
settlement.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.1</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5.1',FILE='C:\fc\898255154_D10466_1943755\9497-1-lo.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 08:02 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Fee payable for the
information technology transition services for 2007 shall be based on the
following:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Global
Applications &amp; Network Services.&#160; </font></i>The
Fee will include: (i) the relevant Employee Costs; (ii) a management fee equal
to 5% of the aggregate amount calculated pursuant to (i); and (iii) third-party
expenses, including travel and entertainment and printing costs, incurred on
behalf of Kraft by ALCS. Direct pass through on any direct charge, i.e.;
circuit charges, routers or monitoring that is currently provided by ALCS or
its contracted third party. This would also include any maintenance and
licensee fee required to maintain Kraft operations until appropriate separation
can be achieved.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Information Technology Contracts
Consulting. </font></i>The Fee shall include: (i) Kraft&#146;s charges under
each information technology contract (primarily AT&amp;T, IBM, Oracle,
Microsoft and SAP contracts), (collectively, the &#147;IT Contracts&#148;), allocated by
usage under the IT Contracts as provided by the service provider; (ii) the
relevant Employee Costs; (iii) a management fee of 5% of the aggregate amount
calculated pursuant to (ii); and (iv) third-party expenses, including travel
and entertainment and printing costs, incurred on behalf of Kraft by ALCS.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.2</font></p>
</div><br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5.2',FILE='C:\fc\898255154_D10466_1943755\9497-1-lo.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 08:02 2007' -->



<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT 6</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">MISCELLANEOUS
SERVICES</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">I.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SPECIFIC TRANSITION SERVICES</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 60.0pt;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>COMPLIANCE</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 78.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Continued operations
under outstanding ALCS agreements with helpline service vendors until no later
than May 15, 2007.</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 78.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ALCS Contracts
Consulting services, if requested by Kraft, related to negotiation of separate
contracts between Kraft and helpline service vendors.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">II.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; SERVICE FEES</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 60.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Fee payable for compliance transition services for 2007 shall include:&#160; (i) Kraft&#146;s charge under each helpline
services contract (if paid by ALCS); (ii) the relevant Employee Costs, if any;
(iii) a management fee of 5% of the aggregate amount calculated pursuant to
(ii); and (iv) any third-party expenses, incurred on behalf of Kraft by ALCS.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.1</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EMPLOYEE MATTERS AGREEMENT</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THIS EMPLOYEE MATTERS AGREEMENT</font></b>, dated as
of March 30, 2007 (as amended and supplemented pursuant to the terms hereof,
this &#147;Agreement&#148;), is entered into by and between Altria Group, Inc., a
Virginia corporation (&#147;Altria&#148;), and Kraft Foods Inc., a Virginia corporation (&#147;Kraft&#148;).</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">W I T N E
S S E T H:</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Altria and Kraft have entered into
a Distribution Agreement, dated as of January 31, 2007 (the &#147;Distribution
Agreement&#148;), providing for, among other things, the distribution by Altria of
its entire ownership interest in Kraft through a pro-rata distribution of all
of the outstanding shares of Class A Common Stock of Kraft owned by Altria on
the Distribution Date to the holders of Altria Common Stock pursuant to the
terms and subject to the conditions of the Distribution Agreement (the &#147;Distribution&#148;);
and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Altria and Kraft wish to set forth
their agreement as to certain matters regarding the treatment of, and the
compensation and employee benefits provided to, employees of Altria and Kraft
and their subsidiaries (as hereinafter defined).</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOW, THEREFORE</font></b>, in consideration of the
premises and the mutual covenants herein contained and intending to be legally
bound hereby, the parties hereto agree as follows:</p>

<h1 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE I<br>
DEFINITIONS</font></b></h1>

<h2 style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><u style="font-weight:bold;">General</u></b>. As used in this Agreement,
the following terms shall have the following meanings (such meanings to be
equally applicable to both the singular and plural forms of the terms defined):</h2>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adjusted
Altria Option</font></u>: an Altria Option as adjusted pursuant to <u>Section
4.1</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Affiliate</font></u>:
with respect to any specified Person, a Person that directly, or indirectly
through one or more intermediaries, controls, is controlled by, or is under
common control with, such specified Person; provided, however, that for
purposes of this Agreement, no member of either Group and no officer or
director of any member of either Group shall be deemed to be an Affiliate of
any member of the other Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria</font></u>:
as defined in the preamble to this Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Benefit Liabilities</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 2.1</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Common Stock</font></u>: the common stock, par value $0.33 1/3 per
share, of Altria.</p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\8982540117_D11265_1943803\9497-1-me.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 08:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Excess Severance Payment</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 3.1(g)(ii)</u>
hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Deferred Stock</font></u>: a deferred stock obligation relating to
Altria Common Stock granted by Altria before the Distribution Date under an
Altria Performance Incentive Plan, but not including any deferred stock granted
by Altria after January 1, 2007 that is held on the Distribution Date by an
employee of the Altria Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Group</font></u>: Altria and the Subsidiaries of Altria other than
members of the Kraft Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Group Employee</font></u>: any individual who (i), as of the close of
business on the Distribution Date, is either employed by, or on a leave of
absence (as defined by the personnel policies of the Altria Group) from, a
member of the Altria Group; (ii) is a Former Altria Group Employee; or (iii) is
or becomes an Altria Transferee.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Group Plans</font></u>:</p>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the Altria Pension
Plans;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the Altria
Profit-Sharing Plans;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the Altria Welfare
and Other Plans; and</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:auto;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; the Altria
Performance Incentive Plans.</font></h4>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria-Kraft
Option</font></u>: an option to acquire Class A Common Stock, granted by
Altria, as of June 12, 2001.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Option</font></u>: an option to acquire Altria Common Stock granted by
Altria under an Altria Performance Incentive Plan before the Distribution Date.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Pension Plans</font></u>: any of the Retirement Plan for Salaried
Employees, the Retirement Plan for Hourly Employees, the Benefit Equalization
Plan, the Supplemental Management Employees&#146; Retirement Plan and any other
qualified or non-qualified defined benefit plan or program that is identified
by Altria before the Distribution Date as providing retirement income to Altria
Group Employees, all as in effect as of the time relevant to the applicable
provisions of this Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Performance Incentive Plans</font></u>: any of the 1992 Incentive
Compensation and Stock Option Plan, the 1997 Performance Incentive Plan, the
2000 Performance Incentive Plan or the 2005 Performance Incentive Plan, or any
stock-based or other incentive plan for Altria Group Employees that is
identified by Altria before the Distribution Date, all as in effect as of the
time relevant to the applicable provisions of this Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Post-Adjustment Price</font></u>: the difference between (i) the Altria
Pre-Adjustment Price and (ii) the Kraft Price multiplied by the Distribution
Ratio.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\8982540117_D11265_1943803\9497-1-me.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 08:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Pre-Adjustment Price</font></u>: the closing price of Altria Common
Stock on the NYSE on the Distribution Date (as traded on the &#147;regular way&#148;
market).</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Profit-Sharing Plan</font></u>: any of the Deferred Profit-Sharing Plan
for Salaried Employees, the Deferred Profit-Sharing Plan for Tobacco Workers,
the Deferred Profit-Sharing Plan for Craft Employees, the Benefit Equalization
Plan, the Supplemental Management Employees&#146; Retirement Plan and any other
qualified or non-qualified defined contribution plan or program for Altria
Group Employees that is identified by Altria before the Distribution Date, all
as in effect as of the time relevant to the applicable provisions of this
Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Restricted Stock</font></u>: restricted Altria Common Stock granted by
Altria before the Distribution Date under an Altria Performance Incentive Plan.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Stock Fund</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 5.1(a)</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Transferee</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 3.2</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Altria
Welfare and Other Plans</font></u>: any plan, fund or program that
provides health, medical, surgical, hospital or dental care or other welfare
benefits or benefits in the event of sickness, accident or disability, or death
benefits to Altria Group Employees, all as in effect as of the time relevant to
the applicable provisions of this Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Arbitration
Act</font></u>: the United States Arbitration Act, 9 U.S.C. &#167;&#167; 1-16, as
the same may be amended from time to time.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Assumed
Altria Pension Plan Liability</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section
3.1(c)</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Assumed
Kraft Pension Plan Liability</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 3.2(c)</u>
hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Auditing
Party</font></u>: as defined in <u>Section 7.3(a)</u> hereof.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Business
Day</font></u>: any day other than a Saturday, a Sunday or a day on
which banking institutions located in the Commonwealth of Virginia or the State
of New York are authorized or obligated by law or executive order to close.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Class
A Common Stock</font></u>: the Class A common stock, no par value, of
Kraft.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Class
B Common Stock</font></u>: the Class B common stock, no par value, of
Kraft.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Code</font></u>:
the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Distribution</font></u>:
as defined in the recitals to this Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Distribution
Date</font></u>: the date on which the Distribution becomes effective.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Distribution
Ratio</font></u>: the fraction determined under Section 2.04(b) of the
Distribution Agreement.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\fc\8982540117_D11265_1943803\9497-1-me.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 30 08:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Equity
Compensation</font></u>: Altria Options, Adjusted Altria Options, Kraft
Options, Altria-Kraft Options, Altria Restricted Stock, Kraft Restricted Stock,
Altria Deferred Stock and Kraft Deferred Stock.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ERISA</font></u>:
Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as amended.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Existing
Kraft Options</font></u>: an option to acquire Class A Common Stock,
granted by Kraft before the Distribution Date under a Kraft Performance
Incentive Plan.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Existing
Kraft Deferred Stock</font></u>: a deferred stock obligation relating to
Class A Common Stock granted by Kraft before the Distribution Date under a
Kraft Performance Incentive Plan.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Existing
Kraft Restricted Stock</font></u>: restricted Class A Common Stock
granted by Kraft before the Distribution Date under a Kraft Performance
Incentive Plan.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fair
Value</font></u>: the anticipated value of the Kraft Options, Adjusted
Altria Options, Altria-Kraft Options or Existing Kraft Options, as applicable,
determined using the Modified Black-Scholes option pricing model used by Altria
and Kraft in the preparation of their most recent respective annual or
quarterly financial reporting prepared before the Distribution Date. Variables
used in the pricing model will be determined as follows:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Expected Life</font></u>: the lesser of two and
one-half years or one-half of the remaining contractual term for each option
grant.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Volatility</font></u>: the annualized
volatilities of Altria or Kraft stock, as applicable, utilizing daily closing
stock prices for the period prior to January 31, 2007 that represents the
Expected Life of each option grant.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adjusted Altria Dividend Yield</font></u>: the
percentage that results from dividing (i) the annualized quarterly dividend per
share of Altria common stock as of the Distribution Date less the value per
Altria share of annualized quarterly dividends on Kraft common stock as of the
Distribution Date by (ii) the Altria Post-Adjustment Price.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Risk-Free Interest Rate</font></u>: the rate
available on the day before the Distribution for zero-coupon U.S. government
securities with terms that approximate the Expected Life of each option grant.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Current Altria and Kraft Stock Prices</font></u>:
the Altria Post-Adjustment Price with respect to Altria Common Stock, and the
Kraft Price with respect to Class A Common Stock.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Former
Altria Group Employee</font></u>: any individual who: (i) before the
Distribution Date has retired from or otherwise separated from service from a
member of the Altria Group; and (ii) still participates in, or otherwise
receives, or is entitled to receive, benefits </p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">under, any Altria
